<text>So I decided to visit this place in Cerritos because it was on the way to a store I was going to.

If you are unsure of dining in right now because of restrictions and want to see someone practicing maximum safety protocol, I recommend this place.

They have a very elaborate operation where you walk inside and up to pre-set ordering tables with menus.  You order what you want and you either choose to eat outside or inside. Me and my partner dined inside and the food was ready amazingly quick.

I ordered Pho noodle soup with rare stake and it was very fresh and tasty. The egg rolls were amazing. The spring rolls! The spam rolls!? The peanut sauce? All amazing.  Like incredible really. The flavors were incredible and everything tasted so fresh. The peanut sauce was thick and creamy and probably the best peanut sauce I have ever had.

Notice the unique serving plates of some of the items as well. It is all part of their elaborate safety protocols to make sure customers have a safe experience during their dining experience.

I recommend this place - I felt a little rushed when ordering - put on the spot even - but the food made me forget about it. Really amazing and delicious vietnamese food.

Go! GO NOW!</text></record>

This is our go-to Pho place near Cerritos.  Prices are good, wait times are typically short and we haven't found a broth we like better.  If you like Pho Tai I recommend getting the beef on the side to avoid having it come out well done.  Just don't wait too long to add it to the soup!

If you are hungry for more than soup get the Cubed Steak with Tomato Rice.  The flavor is among the best of all Vietnamese dishes I have tried.< /Review>

<resp>None<//resp>< text>
I made a horrible mistake coming here a few day ago since there is another pho place in the same shopping center.

The place was empty execept 1 full table of a family. I should have turn aroud and run out then but stupid me just wanted to give it a try.

Even with mostly empty table, the waiter sat me on the table right next to the restroom. Really? Because I came there alone so I wouldnt mind the stench coming from there?

After bringing me the water and the menu. The waiter basically stood there as if I already know what to order right away. I asked for a few minutes to look at the menu. He then realized how awkward the situation was. Even then, all he did was turning around leaning on the next table with the writting pad and pen on his hands. At this point, I really questioned myself whether I should order aome random thing on the menu or continue to figure out a good dish.

So the food came out, the noodle was stale, dry, and very very little. I ordered a plate with shrimp with it came out without even a shell. But to their credit, the food was swallowable.

As I sat their eating, since it was also close to the kitchen, all I could hear was people yelling at each other in the back mixing with some lound pop songs on the speakers. The vibe here guarantees that you will dig through your food quickly.

Needless to say, I left quickly and went to the next door store to buy some additional food to eat. The noodle was that little.<//text>

< username>
Rodney S<//username>
<Time>1475142006905< /Time>< rate>
4< /rate>
< text>
"Where have all the good men gone?
At Pho Little Saigon?
Where's the Viet-wise Hercules?
To eat the steaming pho till it's gone?" - parody of "Holding Out For A Hero", Bonnie Tyler

Formerly Pho Jackie, Pho Little Saigon has been one of my go-to to-go pho places locally.  I'm in the shopping plaza regularly, as I'm usually at the 99 Cent Only store in search of good finds.  After a brisk shopping spree, I headed to Pho Little Saigon for some soul soothing soup.

#2 House Special Combination Pho, large-
With a broth that was light, yet with a distinct taste which I'm unclear as to what it was, the combo pho was nice & plenty in the portion dept.  The various cuts of meat were tender & juicy.  I always ask for extra bean sprouts, and Pho Little Saigon had no problem fulfilling my request.  I was told the wait would be 5 minutes, and my to-go order of pho came out at about the designated time.

Service was good.  I asked and was given water to drink while waiting for my order.  I saw a container of whey protein behind the register and jokingly asked "How much do you charge for a scoop of whey protein powder in my pho?"  Ample seating via handsome bamboo furniture.  Flatscreen TV's available for diner's viewing pleasure.

Parking is at the Artesia Town Centre, which can be packed during the prime hours, shared by Bakers & Baristas, Tampopo, Sweetee Thai & other businesses.

With a lot of options for pho around Cerritos/Artesia, Pho Little Saigon shouldn't be overlooked when you're in search of soup or other Vietnamese dish.  Prices are competitive, and service is friendly & hospitable.  With a 5 minutes turn around for pho, customers can quickly get in & out when pressed for time.  During my next visit, I might just dine in & try one of their highly regarded rice dishes, ending my meal with a refreshing smoothie or 3 bean drink.

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM<//text>

< Review>
I was nicely surprised at the amount of little but thoughtful ideas and details that made my stay very pleasant. Starting with nice pictures on the walls, many lightning options and beautiful lamps, wall electrical outlets in multiple convenient locations. And then gas fireplace, very well equipped kitchen including granite countertop, garburator, dishwasher, dishwashing detergent cube and liquid, scrubbing sponge and brush, and all basic utensils and pans you would need for short stay. Beautiful frameless glass shower with elegant tile job and modern stainless steel linear shower drain. Another granite countertop with sink and beautiful back light mirror.  Admirable attention to details. Even carpets in the halls have an artistic, fresh and colorful design. Add gym and swimming pool with Jacuzzi and it will be tough job to find a better hotel in Sacramento.   Comparing to other hotels offering free breakfast this one was a treat. Altogether very nice, clean and modern hotel with caring and helpful personnel.<//Review>

My family has stayed here 3 times in the last 2 years for a little staycation. Its been almost a year since our last stay and it seems like the quality of product has gone down. They are in the middle of renovations so hopefully the end result will be better.  Let me start by saying the staff is always friendly!!   But we were given an ADA room at checkin which was surprisingly small.  Requested to be moved and and was put in a queen but paid for a king.  Too tired to move again...  was so looking forward to their hot tub to make it all better.  Good thing I came this week because renovations include doing away with the hot tub!!!!  No!!!!!!  There was confusion between the front deck and kitchen on what time breakfast would end since its a holiday.  The food quality was a bit lacking as well.  It just wasnt as smooth a trip as we have come to expect from this property.  Really bummed about the hot tub.  Maybe we will give it another chance after renovations are complete.  Hoping this was just a one off and not the new norm!!!< /review>

< Text>
Melissa and her entire team from house staff to Luay maintenance staff were the model of professionalism to make sure my stay was comfortable and that I felt welcomed. 

This is a very quiet property, and the walls are pretty well insulated such that I couldn‚Äôt hear any noise or conversation from the adjoining rooms. I only heard my neighbors leaving for the day as the room doors are heavy (and thus good for shielding noise). 

I loved the full kitchen, the gas fireplace, and the feel of a separate living and dining area. The workout room is small and basic but had free weights and 2 Precor treadmills. Wish I had brought my swimsuit for the cute indoor pool. 

They have breakfast buffets which I haven‚Äôt tried (I love the privacy of breakfast in my own room, which was nice as they had a toaster and a full set of silverware and dishes for four). 

The rooms may be showing a little bit of wear and age (closet doors came off the tracks, drawers were difficult to open due to warping of the wood) but the consistently thoughtful and warm service puts all of that out of mind.  Love this hotel and will back!< /Text>

<UserId.>None<//UserId.>< text>
Rancho Cordova is a hit or miss area for a safe, quality hotel experience. Residence Inn was an diamond in the middle of the rough I call Rancho Cordova. The hotel staff is amazingly friendly and accommodating, the surroundings are safe and the room was spectacular. You can get a cheaper hotel in the area but the VALUE of your dollar EXCEEDS anything else that you will find.

The rooms were spacious, clean and very functional for your business or pleasure needs (they even have plenty of power outlets built right into the desk so you don't have to re-arrange everything to find an open plug).

The breakfast is one of the best complimentary breakfasts I have ever had at a hotel and the atmosphere is warm, relaxing and inviting.

Close enough to the city that you can make any meetings that you would need to in short order, I would recommend this hotel to anyone who doesn't want to pay the higher rates for being in the city but wants a nice "getaway" spot.</text>

< review>
Great entry to Golden Gate Park. They have walkways for walking or bike riding, roller skating, skate boarding, riding scooter or whatever your fancy. They have a full basketball court with two half side courts, and a workout area. They have a fenced-in little children's playground. They have bathrooms and water dispensaries for both humans, and dogs. Great place for the whole family to enjoy the outdoors.<//review>

< text>
Nice green space with magnificent gum trees and Monterey Cypresses. Provides a much needed break from the concrete jungle. Great bike path, though can be crowded (I still don't understand why people walk on the mixed use path on the north side when the south side has a ped-only path).

The biggest issue is it is surrounded on 2 sides by streets that are nearly freeways, so it's always pretty loud. And getting to the Panhandle usually requires crossing these traffic sewers. The next biggest issue is that Rec and Parks always over-waters grass so the ground is always soaked.<//text>

<Date>1571190454312</Date><rate>5< /rate><Text>The Panhandle is an ideal place to enjoy a pleasant & refreshing moment.  As an eastern extension of Golden Gate Park, it is mostly utilized & appreciated by the locals.
It has a lane for cyclists (Fell Street side)  & one for joggers (Oak Street side).  There is an area for children as well as several basketball courts.  Plenty benches for senior rest stops & acres of lawn for picnics, group activities & other special events.  The landscape is meticulously maintained by Rec & Park.
Hard to believe that back in 60's, the Panhandle was almost paved over in favor of a highway.  The communities fought back & were able to prevail.
Thank goodness.< /Text><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< response>
